id="helping-to-keep-you-safe"><div class="_w_m"><div class="_5aj7 _2auw" id="helping-to-keep-you-safe"><div class="_4bl9">Helping to Keep you Safe</div><div class="_4bl7 _2aux _w_p"><a href="#cs-header">Back to top<i class="_2auy img sp_k6NDE16Bxdr sx_e48816"></i></a></div></div><div class="clearfix _ikh"><div class="_4bl7 _2auz"><i class="img sp_k6NDE16Bxdr id="encouraging-respectful-behavior"><div class="_4bl9">Encouraging respectful behavior</div><div class="_4bl7 _2aux _w_p"><a href="#cs-header">Back to top<i class="_2auy img sp_k6NDE16Bxdr _4-u8" id="keeping-your-account-secure"><div class="_w_m"><div class="_5aj7 _2auw" id="keeping-your-account-secure"><div class="_4bl9">Keeping your account and personal information secure</div><div class="_4bl7 _2aux _w_p"><a href="#cs-header">Back to top<i class="_2auy img sp_k6NDE16Bxdr sx_e48816"></i></a></div></div><div class="clearfix _ikh"><div class="_4bl7 _2auz"><i class="img _2auw" id="protecting-your-intellectual-property"><div class="_4bl9">Protecting your intellectual property</div><div class="_4bl7 _2aux _w_p"><a href="#cs-header">Back to top<i class="_2auy img _55ym _55yq _55yo _3kks" aria-busy="true" role="progressbar" aria-valuemin="0" aria-valuemax="100" aria-valuetext="Loading..."></span></div></div></div></div></div></div><div class="_w_q"><div class="_w_j"><div class="_w_m"><div class="_2auw _3ma">Reporting Abuse</div><div class="_5aj7"><div class="_4bl9 _w_r"> Our global community is growing every day and we strive to welcome people to an environment free from abusive content. To do this, we rely on people like you. If you see something on Facebook that you believe violates our terms, <a href="https://www.facebook.com/help/www/181495968648557">please report it to us</a>. We have dedicated teams working around the world to review things you report to help make sure Facebook remains safe. <br /><br /> Governments also sometimes ask us to remove content that violates local laws, but does not violate our Community Standards. If after careful legal review, we find that the content is illegal under local law, then we may make it unavailable only in the relevant country or territory. <br /><br /> Please keep the following in mind: <br /><br /><ul class="_p7q"><li> We may take action any time something violates the Community Standards outlined here. </li><li> We may ask Page owners to associate their name and Facebook Profile with a Page that contains cruel and insensitive content, even if that content does not violate our policies. </li><li> Reporting something doesn&#039;t guarantee that it will be removed because it may not violate our policies. </li><li> Our content reviewers will look to you for information about why a post may violate our policies. If you report content, please tell us why the content should be removed (e.g., is it nudity or hate speech?) so that we can send it to the right person for review. </li><li> Our review decisions may occasionally change after receiving additional context about specific posts or after seeing new, violating content appearing on a Page or Facebook Profile. </li><li> The number of reports does not impact whether something will be removed. We never remove content simply because it has been reported a number of times. </li><li> The consequences for violating our Community Standards vary depending on the severity of the violation and the person&#039;s history on Facebook. For instance, we may warn someone for a first violation, but if we continue to see further violations we may restrict a person&#039;s ability to post on Facebook or ban the person from Facebook.</li></ul><br /> Not all disagreeable or disturbing content violates our Community Standards. For this reason, we offer you the ability to customize and control what you see by unfollowing, blocking, and hiding the posts, people, Pages, and applications you donât want to see â and we encourage you to use these controls to better personalize your experience. <a href="https://www.facebook.com/help/212722115425932">Learn more</a>. People also often resolve issues they have about a piece of content by simply reaching out to the person who posted it. Weâve created <a href="https://www.facebook.com/help/www/128548343894719">tools</a> for you to communicate directly with other people when youâre unhappy with posts, photos, or other content you see on Facebook. </div><div class="_4bl7 _w_p"><a class="_42ft _4jy0 _55pi _2agf _w_n _4jy3 _4jy2 selected _51sy" role="button" href="/help/181495968648557?ref=community_standards"
